    x.configure(null, adsCfg);
    x.configure("disabledSlots", new Map([ [ "md", [] ], [ "xs", [] ]]));
    x.init();
  });
  godo.ads.push(function(x) {
    x.displayOnScroll({
      threshold: 450,
      delay: 100,
      selector: "[data-ad-lazy=true]"
    });
  });
